                "coverless_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("coverless") or "")),
                "alternate_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("alternate") or "")),
                "subtitle_srt": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("srt") or "")),
                "subtitle_ass": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("ass") or "")),
                "script_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(
                    artifacts_by_id,
                    str(texts.get("script") or subtitles.get("script") or ""),
                ),
                "clip_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(texts.get("clip_text") or "")),
                "cover_image": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(cover.get("image") or "")),
                "forum_post_info": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(context.get("forum_post_info") or "")),
                "processing_log": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(logs.get("processing") or "")),
            },
            "manifest": {
                "primary_artifact_id": render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id"),
                "primary_download_url": render_manifest.get("primary_download_url"),
                "artifact_count": render_manifest.get("artifact_count"),
            },
        }
        return _compact_json_like(openclaw_result)

    def _decorate_task_for_api(task: dict[str, Any], include_openclaw_result: bool = False) -> dict[str, Any]:
        decorated = copy.deepcopy(task)
        task_id = str(decorated.get("task_id") or "").strip()
        if not task_id:
            return decorated

        decorated["status_url"] = _build_status_url(task_id)
        decorated["download_url"] = _build_download_url(task_id)
        decorated["artifacts_url"] = _build_artifacts_url(task_id)
        decorated["openclaw_result_url"] = _build_openclaw_result_url(task_id)

        result = decorated.get("result")
        if not isinstance(result, dict):
            if include_openclaw_result:
                decorated["openclaw_result"] = _build_openclaw_result(decorated)
            return decorated

        artifacts = result.get("artifacts")
        if isinstance(artifacts, list):
            for artifact in artifacts:
                if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
                    continue
                artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
                if artifact_id:
                    artifact["download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, artifact_id)

        render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest")
        if isinstance(render_manifest, dict):
            primary_artifact_id = str(render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") or "").strip()
            if primary_artifact_id:
                render_manifest["primary_download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, primary_artifact_id)
        if include_openclaw_result:
            decorated["openclaw_result"] = _build_openclaw_result(decorated)
        return decorated

    def _save_uploaded_video(task_id: str) -> tuple[Path, str, int]:
        uploaded = request.files.get("file")
        if uploaded is None:
            raise ValueError("missing file field")
        filename = secure_filename(str(uploaded.filename or "").strip()) or "video.mp4"
        suffix = Path(filename).suffix.lower()
        content_type = str(uploaded.content_type or "").strip().lower()
        allowed_suffixes = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
        if suffix and suffix not in allowed_suffixes and not content_type.startswith("video/"):
            raise ValueError(f"unsupported video file type: {suffix or content_type or 'unknown'}")

        task_dir = _api_upload_root / task_id
        task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        target = task_dir / filename
        uploaded.save(str(target))
        size_bytes = target.stat().st_size
        if size_bytes <= 0:
            target.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            raise ValueError("uploaded file is empty")
        return target, filename, size_bytes

    def _build_upload_task_payload(task_id: str, source_path: Path, original_filename: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        payload = _parse_json_object_field("payload")
        metadata = _parse_json_object_field("metadata")
        forum_post_info = _parse_json_object_field("forum_post_info")

        for key in ("clip_text", "stage5_model_name", "stage5_file_encoding", "post_url"):
            value = str(request.form.get(key, "") or "").strip()
            if value:
                payload[key] = value
                metadata[key] = value

        stage5_use_preprocessor = _parse_optional_bool(request.form.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"))
        if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
            payload["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
            metadata["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor

        if forum_post_info:
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info

        metadata.setdefault("source", str(request.form.get("source", "openclaw_upload")).strip() or "openclaw_upload")
        metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
        metadata["uploaded_via"] = "api_multipart"

        task_type = str(request.form.get("task_type", "video") or "video").strip() or "video"
        priority = str(request.form.get("priority", "normal") or "normal").strip() or "normal"

        task_payload: dict[str, Any] = {
            "task_id": task_id,
            "task_type": task_type,
            "priority": priority,
            "source_path": str(source_path),
            "payload": payload,
            "metadata": metadata,
        }

        post_url = str(request.form.get("post_url", "") or "").strip()
        if post_url:
            task_payload["post_url"] = post_url
        return task_payload

    def _require_token(f):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        @wraps(f)
        def decorated(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> Any:
            if not _api_token:
                return f(*args, **kwargs)
            auth = request.headers.get("Authorization", "")
            token = auth.removeprefix("Bearer ").strip() if auth.startswith("Bearer ") else ""
            if not token:
                token = request.args.get("token", "").strip()
            if token != _api_token:
                return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "unauthorized"}), 401
            return f(*args, **kwargs)

        return decorated

    @app.get("/api/tasks")

        try:
            limit = max(1, min(200, int(limit_raw)))
            offset = max(0, int(offset_raw))
        except ValueError:

        try:
            payload = service.list_tasks(status=status, limit=limit, offset=offset)

        tasks = payload.get("tasks") if isinstance(payload.get("tasks"), list) else []
        payload["tasks"] = [_decorate_task_for_api(task) for task in tasks if isinstance(task, dict)]
        return jsonify({"success": True, **payload})

    @app.post("/api/tasks/upload")
    @app.post("/api/tasks/upload-video")
    @_require_token
    def upload_video_task() -> Any:
        requested_task_id = str(request.form.get("task_id", "") or "").strip()
        task_id = requested_task_id or str(uuid.uuid4())
        stored_path: Path | None = None
        stored_dir: Path | None = None
        try:
            stored_path, filename, size_bytes = _save_uploaded_video(task_id=task_id)
            stored_dir = stored_path.parent
            submit_payload = _build_upload_task_payload(
                task_id=task_id,
                source_path=stored_path,
                original_filename=filename,
            )
            ok, resolved_task_id, error = service.submit(submit_payload)
            if not ok:
                raise ValueError(error or "invalid task payload")
        except ValueError as exc:
            if stored_dir is not None and stored_dir.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(stored_dir, ignore_errors=True)
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": str(exc)}), 400
        except Exception as exc:
            if stored_dir is not None and stored_dir.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(stored_dir, ignore_errors=True)
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": f"upload task failed: {exc}"}), 500

        return (
            jsonify(
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                    "filename": filename,
                    "stored_path": str(stored_path),
                    "file_size_bytes": size_bytes,
                    "status_url": f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}",
                    "download_url": f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}/download",
                    "artifacts_url": f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}/artifacts",
                    "openclaw_result_url": f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}/openclaw-result",
                }
            ),
            201,
        )

    @app.get("/api/tasks/<task_id>/download")
    @_require_token
    def task_download(task_id: str) -> Any:
        task = service.get_task(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "task not found"}), 404
        status = str(task.get("status") or "").strip().lower()
        if status not in {"completed", "uploading", "processing"}:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": f"task output not ready: status={status or 'unknown'}"}), 409

        download_path = _resolve_download_path(task)
        if download_path is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "downloadable output not found"}), 404

        return send_file(
            download_path,
            as_attachment=True,
            download_name=download_path.name,
            mimetype="video/mp4",
            conditional=True,
        )

    @app.get("/api/tasks/<task_id>/artifacts/<artifact_id>/download")
    @_require_token
    def task_artifact_download(task_id: str, artifact_id: str) -> Any:
        task = service.get_task(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "task not found"}), 404
        artifact = _find_task_artifact(task, artifact_id)
        if artifact is None:
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "artifact not found"}), 404

        artifact_path = Path(str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip())
        if not artifact_path.exists() or not artifact_path.is_file():
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "artifact file not found"}), 404

        guessed_mime, _ = mimetypes.guess_type(artifact_path.name)
        mime_type = str(artifact.get("mime_type") or guessed_mime or "application/octet-stream")
        return send_file(
            artifact_path,
            as_attachment=True,
            download_name=artifact_path.name,
            mimetype=mime_type,
            conditional=True,
        )

    @app.post("/api/tasks/<task_id>/cancel")
    @_require_token
    def cancel_task(task_id: str) -> Any:
        ok, error = service.cancel_task(task_id)
        if not ok:
            code = 404 if error == "task not found" else 409
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error}), code
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id})

    @app.post("/api/tasks/<task_id>/retry")
    @_require_token
    def retry_task(task_id: str) -> Any:
        ok, error = service.retry_task(task_id)
        if not ok:
            code = 404 if error == "task not found" else 409
            return jsonify({"success": False, "error": error}), code
        return jsonify({"success": True, "task_id": task_id})

    return app


def _run_http(app: Flask, host: str, port: int, logger: logging.Logger) -> None:
    try:
        from waitress import serve

        logger.info("serving with waitress on %s:%s", host, port)
        serve(app, host=host, port=port)
    except Exception:
        logger.info("waitress unavailable, fallback to flask builtin server on %s:%s", host, port)
        app.run(host=host, port=port, debug=False, use_reloader=False)


def main() -> int:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="CloneCut API service")
    parser.add_argument("--port", type=int, default=None, help="override service port")
    parser.add_argument("--host", type=str, default=None, help="override service host")
    parser.add_argument("--config", type=str, default="config/settings.yaml", help="config path")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    cfg = load_app_config(args.config)
    cfg.role = "api"
    cfg.port = args.port or cfg.port
    cfg.host = args.host or cfg.host
    if cfg.redis_namespace == "clonecut_monitor:":
        cfg.redis_namespace = "clonecut_worker:"

    setup_logging(cfg.log_dir, cfg.role)
    logger = logging.getLogger("apps.api")
    logger.info("api booting env=%s host=%s port=%s", cfg.env, cfg.host, cfg.port)

    service = WorkerService(config=cfg, logger=logger)
    embedded_worker_started = _should_start_embedded_worker(cfg)
    if embedded_worker_started:
        logger.info("api embedded worker enabled")
        service.start()
    else:
        logger.info("api embedded worker disabled; expecting dedicated worker service")
    app = create_app(service)
    try:
        _run_http(app, cfg.host, cfg.port, logger)
    finally:
        if embedded_worker_started:
            service.stop()
    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import mimetypes
from pathlib import Path
import time
from typing import Any, Mapping

import requests


def _normalize_api_base(api_base: str) -> str:
    text = str(api_base or "").strip().rstrip("/")
    if not text:
        raise ValueError("api_base is required")
    return text


def _resolve_api_url(api_base: str, path: str) -> str:
    base = _normalize_api_base(api_base)
    suffix = str(path or "").strip()
    if not suffix:
        return base
    if not suffix.startswith("/"):
        suffix = "/" + suffix
    return base + suffix


def _build_auth_headers(api_token: str) -> dict[str, str]:
    token = str(api_token or "").strip()
    if not token:
        return {}
    return {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}"}


def _response_json(response: Any) -> dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        payload = response.json()
    except Exception as exc:
        status_code = getattr(response, "status_code", "unknown")
        text = str(getattr(response, "text", "") or "").strip()
        raise RuntimeError(f"api returned non-json response: status={status_code} body={text}") from exc
    if not isinstance(payload, dict):
        raise RuntimeError(f"api returned invalid payload type: {type(payload)!r}")
    return payload


def _ensure_success_payload(payload: Mapping[str, Any], response: Any, context: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
    body = dict(payload or {})
    if bool(body.get("success")):
        return body
    status_code = getattr(response, "status_code", "unknown")
    error = str(body.get("error") or "").strip() or f"{context} failed"
    raise RuntimeError(f"{context} failed: status={status_code} error={error}")


def _coerce_form_value(value: Any) -> str:
    if isinstance(value, (dict, list)):
        return json.dumps(value, ensure_ascii=False)
    if value is None:
        return ""
    return str(value)


def submit_openclaw_video_task(
    api_base: str,
    video_path: str | Path,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    task_id: str = "",
    source: str = "openclaw_client",
    stage5_model_name: str = "",
    extra_form: Mapping[str, Any] | None = None,
    timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    client = session or requests
    file_path = Path(video_path).expanduser()
    if not file_path.exists() or not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"video file not found: {file_path}")

    form: dict[str, str] = {"source": source}
    if task_id:
        form["task_id"] = str(task_id).strip()
    if stage5_model_name:
        form["stage5_model_name"] = str(stage5_model_name).strip()
    for key, value in dict(extra_form or {}).items():
        text = _coerce_form_value(value)
        if text:
            form[str(key)] = text

    content_type = mimetypes.guess_type(file_path.name)[0] or "application/octet-stream"
    with file_path.open("rb") as file_handle:
        response = client.post(
            _resolve_api_url(api_base, "/api/tasks/upload-video"),
            data=form,
            files={"file": (file_path.name, file_handle, content_type)},
            headers=_build_auth_headers(api_token),
            timeout=max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds)),
        )
    payload = _response_json(response)
    return _ensure_success_payload(payload, response, context="submit openclaw video task")


def fetch_openclaw_result(
    api_base: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    client = session or requests
    resolved_task_id = str(task_id or "").strip()
    if not resolved_task_id:
        raise ValueError("task_id is required")

    response = client.get(
        _resolve_api_url(api_base, f"/api/tasks/{resolved_task_id}/openclaw-result"),
        headers=_build_auth_headers(api_token),
        timeout=max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds)),
    )
    payload = _response_json(response)
    return _ensure_success_payload(payload, response, context="fetch openclaw result")


def wait_for_openclaw_result(
    api_base: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
    poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
    request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    deadline = time.time() + max(1.0, float(timeout_seconds))
    while True:
        payload = fetch_openclaw_result(
            api_base=api_base,
            task_id=task_id,
            api_token=api_token,
            timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
            session=session,
        )
        result = payload.get("openclaw_result") if isinstance(payload.get("openclaw_result"), dict) else {}
        status = str(result.get("status") or "").strip().lower()
        if status in {"completed", "failed", "cancelled"}:
            return payload
        if time.time() >= deadline:
            raise TimeoutError(f"wait openclaw result timed out: task_id={task_id} status={status or 'unknown'}")
        time.sleep(max(0.2, float(poll_interval_seconds)))


def run_openclaw_video_task(
    api_base: str,
    video_path: str | Path,
    *,
    api_token: str = "",
    task_id: str = "",
    source: str = "openclaw_client",
    stage5_model_name: str = "",
    extra_form: Mapping[str, Any] | None = None,
    wait: bool = True,
    submit_timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,
    wait_timeout_seconds: float = 1800.0,
    poll_interval_seconds: float = 5.0,
    request_timeout_seconds: float = 15.0,
    session: Any = None,
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    submitted = submit_openclaw_video_task(
        api_base=api_base,
        video_path=video_path,
        api_token=api_token,
        task_id=task_id,
        source=source,
        stage5_model_name=stage5_model_name,
        extra_form=extra_form,
        timeout_seconds=submit_timeout_seconds,
        session=session,
    )
    output = {"submit": submitted}
    if not wait:
        return output

    resolved_task_id = str(submitted.get("task_id") or "").strip()
    if not resolved_task_id:
        raise RuntimeError("submit response missing task_id")
    output["result"] = wait_for_openclaw_result(
        api_base=api_base,
        task_id=resolved_task_id,
        api_token=api_token,
        timeout_seconds=wait_timeout_seconds,
        poll_interval_seconds=poll_interval_seconds,
        request_timeout_seconds=request_timeout_seconds,
        session=session,
    )
    return output


__all__ = [
    "submit_openclaw_video_task",
    "fetch_openclaw_result",
    "wait_for_openclaw_result",
    "run_openclaw_video_task",
]

def _build_config(tmp_path) -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    ns_hash = hashlib.md5(str(tmp_path).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
    namespace = f"clonecut_worker_unit_{ns_hash}:"
    return SimpleNamespace(
        redis_host="127.0.0.1",
        redis_port=6379,
        redis_db=0,
        redis_password="",
        redis_namespace=namespace,
        input_dir=str(tmp_path / "input"),
        output_dir=str(tmp_path / "output"),
        log_dir=str(tmp_path / "logs"),
        raw={
            "queue": {
                "max_retries": 2,
                "retry_backoff_seconds": [1, 1, 1],
            },
            "worker": {
                "max_download_workers": 1,
                "max_process_workers": 1,
                "max_upload_workers": 1,
                "download_timeout_seconds": 30,
                "download_chunk_size": 4096,
                "tts_enable": True,
                "tts_engine": "local",
                "use_internal_pipeline": False,
                "video_command_template": "",
                "retry_check_interval_seconds": 0.2,
                "zombie_timeout_seconds": 1,
                "zombie_check_interval_seconds": 0.2,
            },
        },
    )


def test_video_task_flows_download_process_upload(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content")

    service.start()
    try:
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
            {
                "task_type": "video",
                "source_url": str(source),
                "metadata": {"source": "unit"},
            }
        )
        assert ok
        assert not error
        assert task_id

        deadline = time.time() + 10
        final_task = None
        while time.time() < deadline:
            final_task = service.get_task(task_id)
            if final_task and final_task.get("status") == "completed":
                break
            time.sleep(0.05)

        assert isinstance(final_task, dict)
        assert final_task.get("status") == "completed"
        assert Path(str(final_task.get("source_path"))).exists()

        result = final_task.get("result")
        assert isinstance(result, dict)
        assert result.get("engine") == "internal_pipeline_auto"
        upload = result.get("upload")
        assert isinstance(upload, dict)
        uploaded_path = upload.get("uploaded_path")
        assert isinstance(uploaded_path, str) and uploaded_path
        assert Path(uploaded_path).exists()
    finally:
        service.stop()


def test_failed_task_auto_retries_until_success(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

    source = tmp_path / "retry-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content")

    original = service._process_video_like
    attempts = {"count": 0}

    def flaky_process(task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        attempts["count"] += 1
        if attempts["count"] == 1:
            raise RuntimeError("inject process failure")
        return original(task)

    service._process_video_like = flaky_process  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service.start()
    try:
        ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
            {
                "task_type": "video",
                "source_url": str(source),
                "metadata": {"source": "retry-test"},
            }
        )
        assert ok
        assert not error

        deadline = time.time() + 15
        final_task = None
        while time.time() < deadline:
            final_task = service.get_task(task_id)
            if final_task and final_task.get("status") == "completed" and attempts["count"] >= 2:
                break
            time.sleep(0.1)

        assert attempts["count"] >= 2
        assert isinstance(final_task, dict)
        assert final_task.get("status") == "completed"
        assert int(final_task.get("retry_count", 0)) >= 1
    finally:
        service.stop()

def test_zombie_task_reclaimed_then_requeued(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    zombie = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="zombie-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "missing.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        current_stage=3,
        stage_checkpoint="stage3_repair",
        max_retries=1,
    )
    zombie.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=40)
    service._persist_task(zombie)

    reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
    assert reclaimed == 1

    time.sleep(1.2)
    ready = service._dequeue_ready_retries()
    assert len(ready) == 1
    service._enqueue_retry_task(ready[0])

    queued = service.queue_adapter.pop_process(timeout=0.1)
    assert queued is not None
    assert queued.task_id == "zombie-1"
    loaded = service.get_task("zombie-1")
    assert isinstance(loaded, dict)
    assert loaded.get("status") == "pending"


def test_zombie_reclaim_uses_status_specific_thresholds(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie_threshold.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["worker"]["zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds"] = {
        "pending": 1,
        "downloading": 120,
        "processing": 120,
        "uploading": 120,
    }
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    pending_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="pending-zombie-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "pending.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
    )
    pending_task.created_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
    service._persist_task(pending_task)

    processing_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="processing-fresh-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_url=str(tmp_path / "processing.mp4"),
        status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
    )
    processing_task.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
    service._persist_task(processing_task)

    reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
    assert reclaimed == 1

    pending_loaded = service.get_task("pending-zombie-1")
    processing_loaded = service.get_task("processing-fresh-1")
    assert isinstance(pending_loaded, dict)
    assert isinstance(processing_loaded, dict)
    assert pending_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.FAILED.value

    no_subtitle_video = task_dir / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰_鏅鸿兘鍓緫鏃犲瓧骞曠増.mp4"
    no_subtitle_video.write_bytes(b"no-subtitle")
    subtitle_srt = task_dir / "total.srt"
    subtitle_srt.write_text("1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nhello\n", encoding="utf-8")
    subtitle_ass = task_dir / "total.ass"
    subtitle_ass.write_text("[Script Info]\n", encoding="utf-8")
    script_text = task_dir / "script.txt"
    script_text.write_text("鍘熷璇嗗埆鏂囨湰", encoding="utf-8")
    clip_text = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
    clip_text.write_text("瑁佸壀鏂囨湰", encoding="utf-8")
    forum_post_info = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
    forum_post_info.write_text('{"thread_id":"123"}', encoding="utf-8")
    cover_image = task_dir / "璁哄潧灏侀潰鏍囬.png"
    cover_image.write_bytes(b"png")
    logs_dir = task_dir / "logs"
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    process_log = logs_dir / "funclip_20260326_150000.log"
    process_log.write_text("pipeline ok", encoding="utf-8")
    state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
    state_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "last_completed_step": 9,
                "output_file": str(final_video),
                "step_name": "鏂囦欢鏁寸悊",
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="render-manifest-task",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
    )
    Path(str(task.source_path)).write_bytes(b"source-video")

    result = service._attach_video_render_manifest(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_video),
        },
    )

    artifacts = result.get("artifacts") or []
    roles = {str(item.get("role")): item for item in artifacts}
    assert "final_video" in roles
    assert roles["final_video"].get("is_primary") is True
    assert "subtitle_srt" in roles
    assert "subtitle_ass" in roles
    assert "clip_text" in roles
    assert "forum_post_info" in roles
    assert "cover_image" in roles
    assert "processing_log" in roles
    assert "pipeline_state" in roles

    render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest") or {}
    assert render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") == roles["final_video"].get("artifact_id")
    subtitles = render_manifest.get("subtitles") or {}
    assert subtitles.get("srt") == roles["subtitle_srt"].get("artifact_id")
    assert subtitles.get("ass") == roles["subtitle_ass"].get("artifact_id")
    texts = render_manifest.get("texts") or {}
    assert texts.get("clip_text") == roles["clip_text"].get("artifact_id")
    assert texts.get("script") == roles["transcript_text"].get("artifact_id")
    context = render_manifest.get("context") or {}
    assert context.get("forum_post_info") == roles["forum_post_info"].get("artifact_id")
    cover = render_manifest.get("cover") or {}
    assert cover.get("image") == roles["cover_image"].get("artifact_id")
    logs = render_manifest.get("logs") or {}
    assert logs.get("processing") == roles["processing_log"].get("artifact_id")
    pipeline_state = render_manifest.get("pipeline_state") or {}
    assert pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step") == 9

    assert info.get("cover_title_up") == "涓婃爣棰?
    assert info.get("cover_title_middle") == "涓爣棰?
    assert info.get("cover_title_down") == "涓嬫爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓婃爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓嬫爣棰?
    assert task.metadata.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"
    assert task.payload.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"

def test_run_process_stage_applies_original_filename_naming(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_naming.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-name-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(source),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "forum_final.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "forum_final.mp4"},
        },
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    stage_output = Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / f"{task.task_id}.mp4"
    stage_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    stage_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    def fake_process_video_like(_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(stage_output),
        }

    enqueued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        enqueued["queue"] = queue_name
        enqueued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._process_video_like = fake_process_video_like  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_process_stage(task)

    assert enqueued.get("queue") == "upload"
    assert enqueued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.output_path is not None
    final_output = Path(task.output_path)
    assert final_output.exists()
    assert final_output.name == "forum_final.mp4"
    assert final_output.read_bytes() == b"processed-video"
    assert stage_output.exists()
    assert task.result is not None
    assert task.result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert task.result.get("original_output_path") == str(stage_output)
    assert task.result.get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_apply_video_output_naming_keeps_equivalent_final_output(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_keep_final.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    final_output = tmp_path / "out" / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛" / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛_final.mp4"
    final_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-keep-final-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4"},
        },
        payload={"original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4"},
    )
    task.source_path and Path(task.source_path).write_bytes(b"video")

    result = service._apply_video_output_naming(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_output),
        },
    )

    assert result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert result.get("named_output_path") is None
    assert not result.get("original_output_path")
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_upload_output_replies_forum_with_strict_attachment(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = logger
            captured["base_url"] = http_client.base_url

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["thread_id"] = thread_id
            captured["content"] = content
            captured["video_files"] = list(video_files)
            captured["strict_attachment"] = bool(strict_attachment)
            return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    upload_result = service._upload_output(task)
    forum_reply = upload_result.get("forum_reply") or {}

    assert upload_result.get("success") is True
    assert upload_result.get("storage") == "local"
    assert forum_reply.get("attempted") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("base_url") == "https://forum.example.com"
    assert captured.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    content = str(captured.get("content") or "")
    assert "馃幀 AI鏅鸿兘鍓緫瀹屾垚锛? in content
    assert "馃摑 鍘熷瑙嗛: 鏈煡鏂囦欢" in content
    assert "馃幆 澶勭悊缁撴灉: 1 涓増鏈? in content
    assert "馃摴 forum-output.mp4" in content
    assert "馃晵 澶勭悊鏃堕棿:" in content
    assert "馃 AI鍓緫鍔╂墜 - 鏅鸿兘瑙嗛澶勭悊瀹屾垚" in content
    assert captured.get("strict_attachment") is True

def test_upload_output_forum_4xx_is_non_retryable(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum_4xx.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output-4xx.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-4xx",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = http_client
            _ = logger

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = thread_id
            _ = content
            _ = video_files
            _ = strict_attachment
            return False, "attachment upload failed: traditional upload failed: status=403"

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    with pytest.raises(NonRetryableUploadError):
        service._upload_output(task)


def test_fail_task_skips_retry_for_non_retryable_upload_error(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_non_retryable.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-no-retry-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        status=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        max_retries=2,
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    service._fail_task(
        task=task,
        error=NonRetryableUploadError("attachment upload failed: status=403"),
        failed_from=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
    )

    assert task.status == TaskStatus.FAILED
    assert task.retry_count == 0
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure") is False
    assert "retry_due_at" not in (task.metadata or {})


def test_retry_delay_uses_upload_backoff_series(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_backoff.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["queue"]["retry_backoff_seconds"] = [9, 9, 9]
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    upload_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value},
    )
    process_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="process-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value},
    )

    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 0) == 1
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 1) == 2
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 2) == 4
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(process_task, 0) == 9


def test_run_download_stage_parses_forum_post_and_writes_forum_info_snapshot(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_parse_download.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source_media = tmp_path / "post-source.mp4"
    source_media.write_bytes(b"forum-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-parse-download-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_url="https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html",
        status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
        metadata={"source": "forum"},
        payload={},
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    parsed_called: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_parse(post_url):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        parsed_called["post_url"] = post_url
        return {
            "post_url": post_url,
            "thread_id": "9876",
            "post_id": "9876",
            "video_url": str(source_media),
            "video_urls": [str(source_media)],
            "original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4",
            "title": "forum title",
            "author_name": "alice",
        }

    queued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        queued["queue"] = queue_name
        queued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._resolve_forum_post_download_info = fake_parse  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_download_stage(task)

    assert parsed_called.get("post_url") == "https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html"
    assert queued.get("queue") == "process"
    assert queued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.source_path is not None
    downloaded_path = Path(task.source_path)
    assert downloaded_path.exists()
    assert downloaded_path.name == "forum_topic.mp4"
    assert downloaded_path.read_bytes() == b"forum-video"
    info_path = Path(str((task.metadata or {}).get("forum_post_info_path", "")))
    assert info_path.exists()
    snapshot = info_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert '"thread_id": "9876"' in snapshot
    assert '"original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4"' in snapshot

from pathlib import Path

import pytest

from apps.api.openclaw_client import run_openclaw_video_task, submit_openclaw_video_task, wait_for_openclaw_result


class _FakeResponse:
    def __init__(self, status_code: int, payload):
        self.status_code = status_code
        self._payload = payload
        self.text = str(payload)

    def json(self):
        return self._payload


class _FakeSession:
    def __init__(self, post_responses=None, get_responses=None) -> None:
        self.post_responses = list(post_responses or [])
        self.get_responses = list(get_responses or [])
        self.post_calls = []
        self.get_calls = []

    def post(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        self.post_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
        if not self.post_responses:
            raise AssertionError("unexpected post call")
        return self.post_responses.pop(0)

    def get(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        self.get_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
        if not self.get_responses:
            raise AssertionError("unexpected get call")
        return self.get_responses.pop(0)


def test_submit_openclaw_video_task_posts_expected_form(tmp_path) -> None:
    video = tmp_path / "sample.mp4"
    video.write_bytes(b"video")
    session = _FakeSession(
        post_responses=[
            _FakeResponse(
                201,
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": "task-123",
                    "openclaw_result_url": "/api/tasks/task-123/openclaw-result",
                },
            )
        ]
    )

    payload = submit_openclaw_video_task(
        api_base="http://127.0.0.1:18100",
        video_path=video,
        api_token="token-1",
        stage5_model_name="yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4",
        extra_form={"metadata": {"source": "test"}},
        session=session,
    )

    assert payload.get("task_id") == "task-123"
    call = session.post_calls[0]
    assert call["url"] == "http://127.0.0.1:18100/api/tasks/upload-video"
    assert call["headers"]["Authorization"] == "Bearer token-1"
    assert call["data"]["stage5_model_name"] == "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"
    assert call["data"]["metadata"] == '{"source": "test"}'
    uploaded_name, _, uploaded_content_type = call["files"]["file"]
    assert uploaded_name == "sample.mp4"
    assert uploaded_content_type == "video/mp4"


def test_wait_for_openclaw_result_polls_until_completed(monkeypatch) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    session = _FakeSession(
        get_responses=[
            _FakeResponse(
                200,
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": "task-123",
                    "openclaw_result": {"status": "processing"},
                },
            ),
            _FakeResponse(
                200,
                {
                    "success": True,
                    "task_id": "task-123",
                    "openclaw_result": {"status": "completed", "outputs": {"final_video": {"artifact_id": "final"}}},
                },
            ),
        ]
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.api.openclaw_client.time.sleep", lambda _seconds: None)

    payload = wait_for_openclaw_result(
        api_base="http://127.0.0.1:18100",
        task_id="task-123",
        poll_interval_seconds=0.2,
        session=session,
    )

    assert payload.get("openclaw_result", {}).get("status") == "completed"
    assert len(session.get_calls) == 2

from domain.task.models import TaskStatus, TaskType, UnifiedTask


def _build_config(tmp_path) -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    return SimpleNamespace(
        redis_host="127.0.0.1",
        redis_port=6379,
        redis_db=0,
        redis_password="",
        redis_namespace="clonecut_api_integration:",
        input_dir=str(tmp_path / "input"),
        output_dir=str(tmp_path / "output"),
        log_dir=str(tmp_path / "logs"),
        raw={
            "queue": {
                "max_retries": 2,
                "retry_backoff_seconds": [1, 1, 1],
            },
            "worker": {
                "max_download_workers": 1,
                "max_process_workers": 1,
                "max_upload_workers": 1,
                "download_timeout_seconds": 30,
                "download_chunk_size": 4096,
                "use_internal_pipeline": False,
                "video_command_template": "",
            },
        },
    )


def test_api_task_lifecycle_list_and_cancel(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "api_lifecycle.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    app = create_app(service)
    client = app.test_client()

    source = tmp_path / "task-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")

    created = client.post(
        "/api/tasks",
        json={
            "task_type": "video",
            "source_url": str(source),
            "metadata": {"source": "api-test"},
        },
    )
    assert created.status_code == 201
    created_payload = created.get_json() or {}
    task_id = str(created_payload.get("task_id", "")).strip()
    assert task_id

    listed = client.get("/api/tasks", query_string={"status": "pending", "limit": 20, "offset": 0})
    assert listed.status_code == 200
    listed_payload = listed.get_json() or {}
    assert listed_payload.get("success") is True
    tasks = listed_payload.get("tasks") or []
    assert any(str(item.get("task_id")) == task_id for item in tasks)

    cancelled = client.post(f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/cancel")
    assert cancelled.status_code == 200
    cancelled_payload = cancelled.get_json() or {}
    assert cancelled_payload.get("success") is True

    detail = client.get(f"/api/tasks/{task_id}")
    assert detail.status_code == 200
    detail_payload = detail.get_json() or {}
    assert detail_payload.get("success") is True
    task_payload = detail_payload.get("task") or {}
    assert task_payload.get("status") == TaskStatus.CANCELLED.value

    queue_status = client.get("/api/queues")
    assert queue_status.status_code == 200
    queue_payload = queue_status.get_json() or {}
    counts = queue_payload.get("task_status_counts") or {}
    assert int(counts.get(TaskStatus.CANCELLED.value, 0)) >= 1


def test_api_retry_failed_task(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "api_retry.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    app = create_app(service)
    client = app.test_client()

    source = tmp_path / "failed-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    failed = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="failed-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="api-test",
        source_path=str(source),
        status=TaskStatus.FAILED,
        metadata={
            "source": "api-test",
            "failed_from_status": TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value,
        },
    )
    service._persist_task(failed)

    retried = client.post("/api/tasks/failed-1/retry")
    assert retried.status_code == 200
    retried_payload = retried.get_json() or {}
    assert retried_payload.get("success") is True

    detail = client.get("/api/tasks/failed-1")
    assert detail.status_code == 200
    detail_payload = detail.get_json() or {}
    task_payload = detail_payload.get("task") or {}
    assert task_payload.get("status") == TaskStatus.PENDING.value
    metadata = task_payload.get("metadata") or {}
    assert metadata.get("manual_retry") is True

    queue_status = client.get("/api/queues")
    assert queue_status.status_code == 200
    queue_payload = queue_status.get_json() or {}
    queue_sizes = queue_payload.get("queue_sizes") or {}
    assert int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0)) >= 1


def test_api_tasks_invalid_status_filter_returns_400(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "api_invalid_status.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    app = create_app(service)
    client = app.test_client()

    response = client.get("/api/tasks", query_string={"status": "not-a-status"})
    assert response.status_code == 400
    payload = response.get_json() or {}
    assert payload.get("success") is False


def test_api_task_artifacts_list_and_download(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "api_artifacts.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    app = create_app(service)
    client = app.test_client()

    task_dir = Path(cfg.output_dir) / "artifact-task-1"
    task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_video = task_dir / "artifact-task-1_final.mp4"
    final_video.write_bytes(b"video")
    subtitle_srt = task_dir / "total.srt"
    subtitle_srt.write_text("1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nhello\n", encoding="utf-8")
    clip_text = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
    clip_text.write_text("鍓緫鏂囨湰", encoding="utf-8")
    forum_post_info = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
    forum_post_info.write_text('{"thread_id":"123"}', encoding="utf-8")
    cover_image = task_dir / "artifact-cover.png"
    cover_image.write_bytes(b"png")
    logs_dir = task_dir / "logs"
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (logs_dir / "funclip_20260326_150000.log").write_text("ok", encoding="utf-8")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="artifact-task-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="api-test",
        status=TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
        output_path=str(final_video),
    )
    Path(str(task.source_path)).write_bytes(b"source")
    task.result = service._attach_video_render_manifest(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_video),
        },
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    detail = client.get("/api/tasks/artifact-task-1")
    assert detail.status_code == 200
    detail_payload = detail.get_json() or {}
    task_payload = detail_payload.get("task") or {}
    assert task_payload.get("artifacts_url") == "/api/tasks/artifact-task-1/artifacts"
    assert task_payload.get("openclaw_result_url") == "/api/tasks/artifact-task-1/openclaw-result"
    result = task_payload.get("result") or {}
    artifacts = result.get("artifacts") or []
    assert artifacts
    subtitle_artifact = next(item for item in artifacts if item.get("role") == "subtitle_srt")
    clip_text_artifact = next(item for item in artifacts if item.get("role") == "clip_text")
    assert subtitle_artifact.get("download_url") == (
        f"/api/tasks/artifact-task-1/artifacts/{subtitle_artifact.get('artifact_id')}/download"
    )
    assert task_payload.get("openclaw_result", {}).get("outputs", {}).get("clip_text", {}).get("artifact_id") == (
        clip_text_artifact.get("artifact_id")
    )

    listed = client.get("/api/tasks/artifact-task-1/artifacts")
    assert listed.status_code == 200
    listed_payload = listed.get_json() or {}
    listed_artifacts = listed_payload.get("artifacts") or []
    assert any(item.get("role") == "cover_image" for item in listed_artifacts)

    subtitle_download = client.get(subtitle_artifact.get("download_url"))
    assert subtitle_download.status_code == 200
    assert b"hello" in subtitle_download.data

    openclaw_result_resp = client.get("/api/tasks/artifact-task-1/openclaw-result")
    assert openclaw_result_resp.status_code == 200
    openclaw_result_payload = openclaw_result_resp.get_json() or {}
    openclaw_result = openclaw_result_payload.get("openclaw_result") or {}
    outputs = openclaw_result.get("outputs") or {}
    assert outputs.get("final_video", {}).get("filename") == "artifact-task-1_final.mp4"
    assert outputs.get("subtitle_srt", {}).get("artifact_id") == subtitle_artifact.get("artifact_id")
    assert outputs.get("clip_text", {}).get("artifact_id") == clip_text_artifact.get("artifact_id")
    assert outputs.get("forum_post_info", {}).get("filename") == "forum_post_info.json"
    assert outputs.get("processing_log", {}).get("filename") == "funclip_20260326_150000.log"

 1582:     def _normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(self, model_name: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str]]:
 1583:         raw_model = str(model_name or "").strip()
 1584:         if not raw_model:
 1585:             return "", None
 1586: 
 1587:         normalized = raw_model.lower()
 1588:         supported = {"openai", "qwen", "g4f", "deepseek", "kimi"}
 1589:         if normalized in supported:
 1590:             return normalized, None
 1591: 
 1592:         # Old stage5 only accepts provider ids. Route custom backend model ids
 1593:         # through the OpenAI-compatible adapter and pass the real backend via env.
 1594:         return "openai", raw_model

 1596:     def _collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs(self) -> List[str]:
 1597:         tool_dirs: List[str] = []
 1598: 
 1599:         explicit_dir = str(
 1600:             os.getenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "") or os.getenv("FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "")
 1601:         ).strip()
 1602:         if explicit_dir:
 1603:             candidate = Path(explicit_dir).expanduser().resolve()
 1604:             if candidate.exists():
 1605:                 tool_dirs.append(str(candidate))
 1606: 
 1607:         base_prefix = str(getattr(sys, "base_prefix", "") or "").strip()
 1608:         if base_prefix:
 1609:             prefix_path = Path(base_prefix).resolve()
 1610:             sibling_ffmpeg_dir = prefix_path.parent / "ffmpeg" / "bin"
 1611:             if sibling_ffmpeg_dir.exists():
 1612:                 tool_dirs.append(str(sibling_ffmpeg_dir))
 1613:

 1615:         seen: set[str] = set()
 1616:         for item in tool_dirs:
 1617:             normalized = str(item).strip()
 1618:             if normalized and normalized not in seen:
 1619:                 seen.add(normalized)
 1620:                 deduped.append(normalized)
 1621:         return deduped

 1649:     def _build_internal_pipeline_env(self, pipeline_inputs: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:
 1650:         env = dict(os.environ)
 1651:         path_entries: List[str] = []
 1652: 
 1653:         python_scripts_dir = Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent
 1654:         if python_scripts_dir.exists():
 1655:             path_entries.append(str(python_scripts_dir))
 1656: 
 1657:         path_entries.extend(self._collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs())
 1658: 
 1659:         current_path = str(env.get("PATH", "") or "")
 1660:         if current_path:
 1661:             path_entries.append(current_path)
 1662:         env["PATH"] = os.pathsep.join(path_entries)
 1663: 
 1664:         # Keep legacy pipeline subprocess I/O stable on Windows even when old
 1665:         # Rich logs emit emoji or non-ASCII text.
 1666:         env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"

 1670:         if isinstance(pipeline_inputs, dict):

 1672:         if backend_model:

 1676:     def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
 1677:         state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
 1678:         if not state_file.exists():
 1679:             raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
 1680:         try:
 1681:             payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 1682:         except Exception as exc:
 1683:             raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc
 1684: 
 1685:         last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
 1686:         if last_completed_step < 9:
 1687:             raise RuntimeError(
 1688:                 f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
 1689:             )
 1690:         output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
 1691:         if output_file:
 1692:             candidate = Path(output_file)
 1693:             if candidate.exists():
 1694:                 return candidate
 1695: 
 1696:         patterns = [
 1697:             f"{source_path.stem}*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
 1698:             "*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
 1699:             "*.mp4",
 1700:         ]
 1701:         for pattern in patterns:
 1702:             candidates = [
 1703:                 p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
 1704:                 if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
 1705:             ]
 1706:             if candidates:
 1707:                 candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
 1708:                 return candidates[0]
 1709: 
 1710:         raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")

 1712:     def _run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
 1713:         self,
 1714:         task: UnifiedTask,
 1715:         source: Path,
 1716:         task_dir: Path,
 1717:         stage_names: List[str],
 1718:         start_from_stage: int,

 1729:                 [
 1730:                     "1",

 1732:                     "internal pipeline fallback subtitle",
 1733:                     "",

 1746:                 },
 1747:                 ensure_ascii=False,
 1748:                 indent=2,
 1749:             ),
 1750:             encoding="utf-8",
 1751:         )
 1752: 
 1753:         executed = stage_names[start_from_stage:]
 1754:         task.current_stage = len(stage_names) - 1
 1755:         task.stage_checkpoint = stage_names[-1]
 1756:         return {
 1757:             "success": True,
 1758:             "request_type": task.task_type.value,
 1759:             "output_path": str(output_path),
 1760:             "executed_stages": executed,

 1762:             "performance_summary": (
 1763:                 f"internal pipeline fallback executed stages={len(executed)} reason={reason}"
 1764:             ),
 1765:         }

 2120:     def _should_expose_video_artifact(self, path: Path) -> bool:
 2121:         suffix = path.suffix.lower()
 2122:         name = path.name.lower()
 2123:         video_exts = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
 2124:         image_exts = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}
 2125:         if suffix in video_exts or suffix in image_exts:
 2126:             return True
 2127:         if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass", "script.txt", "state.json"}:
 2128:             return True
 2129:         if name in {"clip_text.txt", "forum_post_info.json"}:
 2130:             return True
 2131:         if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in name:
 2132:             return True
 2133:         if suffix == ".log":
 2134:             return True
 2135:         return False

 2137:     def _classify_video_artifact_role(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
 2138:         text = path.name.lower()
 2139:         suffix = path.suffix.lower()
 2140:         if primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved:
 2141:             return "final_video", "video"
 2142:         if text == "total.srt":
 2143:             return "subtitle_srt", "subtitle"
 2144:         if text == "total.ass":
 2145:             return "subtitle_ass", "subtitle"
 2146:         if text == "script.txt":
 2147:             return "transcript_text", "transcript"
 2148:         if text == "clip_text.txt":
 2149:             return "clip_text", "text"

import json
from pathlib import Path

from domain.video import VideoPipeline, VideoPipelineConfig
from domain.video.stages.base import StageResult


def test_internal_pipeline_skeleton_runs(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(input_video=str(source), task_id="video-1")

    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file is not None
    assert Path(result.output_file).exists()
    assert "stage0_clean" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage1_transcode" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage2_silence" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage3_repair" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage4_asr" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage5_ai_text" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage6_clip" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage6_5_resub" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage7_correct" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage7_subtitle" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage8_cover" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage9_organize" in result.executed_stages
    assert result.current_stage == 11
    assert result.failed_stage is None
    srt = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    missing = tmp_path / "missing.mp4"

    result = pipeline.run(input_video=str(missing), task_id="video-2", start_from_stage=1)
    assert not result.success
    assert result.failed_stage == "stage1_transcode"
    assert result.current_stage == 1


def test_pipeline_stage4_manifest_contains_forum_context(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "shared.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "pipeline context subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", str(sidecar))

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        task_id="video-ctx",
        forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["topic-a", "topic-b"], "speaker": "spk-1"},
    )

    assert result.success
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-ctx" / "_stages" / "video-ctx_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("hotwords") == ["topic-a", "topic-b"]
    assert payload.get("hotword_count") == 2
    assert payload.get("speaker") == "spk-1"

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def run_stage5_ai_text(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    task_root = Path(output_dir) / task_id
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage5 input missing")

    script_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_ai_script", ".txt")
    pointer_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_script_path", ".txt")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_ai_manifest", ".json")
    clip_text_path = task_root / "clip_text.txt"
    script_text = "Script Draft\n\nKey Points:\n- skeleton output\n"
    script_path.write_text(script_text, encoding="utf-8")
    clip_text_path.write_text(script_text, encoding="utf-8")
    pointer_path.write_text(str(script_path), encoding="utf-8")
    use_forum_keywords = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_USE_FORUM_KEYWORDS", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
    hotwords = []
    raw_hotwords = forum_post_info.get("hotwords", []) if isinstance(forum_post_info, dict) else []
    if use_forum_keywords:
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for item in raw_hotwords:
            text = str(item).strip()
            if not text or text in seen:
                continue
            seen.add(text)
            hotwords.append(text)
    llm_use_factory = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_USE_FACTORY", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    llm_provider = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_PROVIDER", "rule").strip().lower()
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    engine = "rule_based"
    llm_error = ""
    fallback_used = False
    strict_rejected = False
    if llm_use_factory and llm_provider == "rule":
        engine = "llm_factory:rule"
    elif llm_use_factory and llm_provider != "rule":
        engine = "rule_based"
        llm_error = "missing api_key for provider"
        fallback_used = True
        if strict:
            strict_rejected = True

    manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "task_id": task_id,
                "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
                "engine": engine,
                "keywords": hotwords,
                "use_forum_keywords": use_forum_keywords,
                "forum_keyword_count": len(hotwords),
                "llm_use_factory": llm_use_factory,
                "llm_error": llm_error,
                "fallback_used": fallback_used,
                "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
            indent=2,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    if strict_rejected:
        return StageResult(
            success=False,
            output_file=str(source),
            error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage5 fallback",
            artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)},
        )
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(source), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage5_ai_text(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
import shutil
import subprocess
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, probe_duration_seconds, stage_artifact_path


def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None


def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _build_clip_ranges(
    *,
    subtitle_path: Path,
    video_duration: float,
    max_duration: float = 0.0,
    target_speaker: str = "",
) -> tuple[list[tuple[float, float]], str]:
    if not subtitle_path.exists():
        return ([(0.0, max(0.1, float(video_duration or 1.0)))], "merged=1 missing_subtitle")
    text = subtitle_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    # Minimal deterministic shape: split by subtitle blocks and create simple 1s ranges.
    blocks = [item for item in text.split("\n\n") if item.strip()]
    ranges: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
    matched = 0
    total = 0
    cursor = 0.0
    for block in blocks:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in block.splitlines() if line.strip()]
        if len(lines) < 3:
            continue
        total += 1
        content = " ".join(lines[2:]).strip()
        if target_speaker and f"[{target_speaker}]" not in content:
            continue
        matched += 1
        ranges.append((cursor, min(cursor + 1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0))))
        cursor += 1.5
    if not ranges:
        ranges = [(0.0, min(1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0)))]
    if max_duration and max_duration > 0:
        limited: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
        spent = 0.0
        for start, end in ranges:
            dur = max(0.0, end - start)
            if spent + dur <= max_duration:
                limited.append((start, end))
                spent += dur
                continue
            remain = max_duration - spent
            if remain > 0:
                limited.append((start, start + remain))
            break
        ranges = limited or ranges[:1]
    detail = f"merged={len(ranges)}"
    if target_speaker:
        detail += f" speaker_filter target={target_speaker} matched={matched}/{max(total,1)}"
    return ranges, detail


def _render_trim_seconds(source: Path, target: Path, target_seconds: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    codec = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip() or os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip()
    codec = codec or "libx264"
    cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", codec, str(target)]
    ok, err = run_ffmpeg(cmd)
    if ok:
        return True, ""
    if codec.endswith("_nvenc") and "nvenc" in err.lower():
        cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", "libx264", str(target)]
        return run_ffmpeg(cmd)
    return False, err


def _resolve_clip_text_input(output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    env_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_PATH", "").strip()
    candidate_paths: list[Path] = []
    if env_path:
        candidate_paths.append(Path(env_path))
    candidate_paths.append(Path(output_dir) / task_id / "clip_text.txt")

    for path in candidate_paths:
        if not path.exists() or not path.is_file():
            continue
        try:
            return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), str(path)
        except Exception:
            continue
    return "", ""


def run_stage6_clip(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage6 input missing")

    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip_manifest", ".json")
    out_copy = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip_copy", ".mp4")
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    payload: dict[str, Any] = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "method": "copy_fallback",
        "fallback_used": False,
        "strict_rejected": False,
        "detail": "",
    }

    guide_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH", "").strip()
    clip_text_match = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MATCH", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    subtitle_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
    stage4_manifest = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")
    target_speaker = ""
    if stage4_manifest.exists():
        try:
            target_speaker = str(json.loads(stage4_manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8")).get("speaker", "")).strip()
        except Exception:
            target_speaker = ""

    if ffmpeg_exists():
        out_clip = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip", ".mp4")
        if guide_path:
            seconds = probe_duration_seconds(guide_path)
            ok, err = _render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=out_clip, target_seconds=max(0.1, seconds))
            if ok:
                payload["method"] = "duration_guide_trim"
                manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
            payload["error"] = err
        elif clip_text_match:
            clip_text, clip_text_source = _resolve_clip_text_input(output_dir=output_dir, task_id=task_id)
            payload["clip_text_used"] = bool(clip_text.strip())
            payload["clip_text_source"] = clip_text_source
            if not payload["clip_text_used"]:
                payload["fallback_used"] = True
                payload["detail"] = "clip_text_missing"
                if strict:
                    payload["method"] = "strict_rejected"
                    payload["strict_rejected"] = True
                    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                    return StageResult(
                        success=False,
                        output_file=str(source),
                        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage6 clip_text fallback",
                    )
                ranges, detail = _build_clip_ranges(
                    subtitle_path=subtitle_path,
                    video_duration=max(1.0, probe_duration_seconds(input_video)),
                    max_duration=0.0,
                    target_speaker=target_speaker,
                )
                payload["detail"] = f"{payload['detail']} {detail}".strip()
                ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-c", "copy", str(out_clip)])
                if ok:
                    payload["method"] = "subtitle_concat"
                    payload["ranges"] = ranges
                    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
                payload["error"] = err
                payload["method"] = "copy_fallback"
            else:
                ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-c", "copy", str(out_clip)])
                if ok:
                    payload["method"] = "subtitle_clip_text_concat"
                    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
                payload["error"] = err
        else:
            ranges, detail = _build_clip_ranges(
                subtitle_path=subtitle_path,
                video_duration=max(1.0, probe_duration_seconds(input_video)),
                max_duration=0.0,
                target_speaker=target_speaker,
            )
            payload["detail"] = detail
            ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-c", "copy", str(out_clip)])
            if ok:
                payload["method"] = "subtitle_concat" if target_speaker else "subtitle_concat"
                payload["ranges"] = ranges
                manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
            payload["error"] = err

    payload["fallback_used"] = True
    if strict:
        payload["method"] = "strict_rejected"
        payload["strict_rejected"] = True
        manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=str(source), error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage6 fallback")

    shutil.copyfile(source, out_copy)
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_copy))


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage6_clip(*args, **kwargs)

import json
