from typing import Any
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None


def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _render_title_overlay_image(output_path: str, width: int, height: int, lines: list[str]) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    # Deterministic placeholder image artifact for compatibility-only phase.
    payload = f"overlay {width}x{height} {' | '.join(lines)}".encode("utf-8")
    Path(output_path).write_bytes(payload)
    return True, ""


def run_stage8_cover(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage8 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_cover_titles = info.get("cover_titles") if isinstance(info.get("cover_titles"), list) else []
    cover_titles: list[str] = []
    for item in raw_cover_titles:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        if text:
            cover_titles.append(text)
    if not cover_titles:
        for key in ("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?):
            text = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
            if text:
                cover_titles.append(text)

    title_txt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_title", ".txt")
    title_txt.write_text("\n".join(cover_titles) + ("\n" if cover_titles else ""), encoding="utf-8")
    output_video = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover", ".mp4")
    overlay_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_overlay", ".png")
    subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    if not subtitle_for_timing.exists():
        subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")

    method = "title_text_only"
    overlay_duration_seconds = 0.0
    fallback_used = False
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    if ffmpeg_exists():
        _render_title_overlay_image(str(overlay_path), 1280, 720, cover_titles)
        overlay_duration_seconds = 1.7 if subtitle_for_timing.exists() else 2.0
        filter_expr = f"[0:v][1:v]overlay=0:0:enable='between(t,0,{overlay_duration_seconds:.3f})'"
        ok, err = run_ffmpeg(
            ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-i", str(overlay_path), "-filter_complex", filter_expr, str(output_video)]
        )
        if ok and output_video.exists():
            method = "video_title_overlay"
        else:
            fallback_used = True
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)
    else:
        fallback_used = True
        if strict:
            method = "strict_rejected"
        else:
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)

    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "cover_titles": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_lines": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_up": str(info.get("cover_title_up", "")),
        "cover_title_middle": str(info.get("cover_title_middle", "")),
        "cover_title_down": str(info.get("cover_title_down", "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "method": method,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
        "overlay_duration_seconds": overlay_duration_seconds,
    }
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_manifest", ".json")
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(
        success=not strict_rejected,
        output_file=str(output_video if output_video.exists() else source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage8 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path), "title_file": str(title_txt)},
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage8_cover(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path
from types import SimpleNamespace

import apps.worker.service as worker_service_module
from apps.worker.service import WorkerService
from domain.task.models import TaskType, UnifiedTask


def _build_config(tmp_path, *, runner_mode: str = "subprocess") -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    return SimpleNamespace(
        redis_host="127.0.0.1",
        redis_port=6379,
        redis_db=0,
        redis_password="",
        redis_namespace="clonecut_worker_test:",
        input_dir=str(tmp_path / "input"),
        output_dir=str(tmp_path / "output"),
        log_dir=str(tmp_path / "logs"),
        raw={
            "queue": {
                "max_retries": 1,
                "retry_backoff_seconds": [1],
            },
            "worker": {
                "max_download_workers": 1,
                "max_process_workers": 1,
                "max_upload_workers": 1,
                "use_internal_pipeline": True,
                "internal_pipeline_runner": runner_mode,
                "internal_pipeline_pool_size": 1,
                "internal_pipeline_warmup_on_start": False,
                "video_command_template": "",
            },
        },
    )


def _build_task(source: Path) -> UnifiedTask:
    return UnifiedTask(
        task_id="video-task-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit-test",
        source_path=str(source),
        payload={},
        metadata={},
    )


def test_worker_service_start_and_stop_controls_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "runner_lifecycle.db"))
    events: list[str] = []

    class FakeRunner:
        def __init__(self, **_kwargs) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            events.append("runner_init")

        def start(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_start")

        def stop(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_stop")

    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "InternalPipelineWarmRunner", FakeRunner)

    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path, runner_mode="warm_process"))
    service.resource_monitor = SimpleNamespace(
        start=lambda: events.append("resource_start"),
        stop=lambda: events.append("resource_stop"),
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_recover_stuck_tasks", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_restore_retry_schedule", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_spawn_workers", lambda *_args, **_kwargs: None)

    service.start()
    service.stop()

    assert events == [
        "runner_init",
        "runner_start",
        "resource_start",
        "runner_stop",
        "resource_stop",
    ]


def test_run_internal_pipeline_prefers_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "warm_success.db"))
    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path))

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    expected_output = Path(service.config.output_dir) / "video-task-1" / "final.mp4"
    expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    expected_output.write_bytes(b"done")

    warm_calls: list[dict] = []

    class FakeRunner:
        def execute(self, *, payload, timeout_seconds):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            warm_calls.append({"payload": payload, "timeout_seconds": timeout_seconds})
            return {"success": True}

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FakeRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path", lambda **_kwargs: expected_output)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        worker_service_module.subprocess,
        "run",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("subprocess should not run")),
    )

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))

    assert len(warm_calls) == 1
    assert warm_calls[0]["payload"]["input_path"] == str(source)
    assert result["output_path"] == str(expected_output)
    assert "backend=warm_process" in str(result["performance_summary"])


def test_run_internal_pipeline_falls_back_to_subprocess_when_warm_runner_fails(
    monkeypatch,
    tmp_path,
) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "warm_fallback.db"))
    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path))

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    expected_output = Path(service.config.output_dir) / "video-task-1" / "fallback.mp4"
    expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    expected_output.write_bytes(b"done")

    class FailingRunner:
        def execute(self, *, payload, timeout_seconds):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            raise RuntimeError("warm failed")

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FailingRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module.importlib.util, "find_spec", lambda _name: object())
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path", lambda **_kwargs: expected_output)

    class FakeCompletedProcess:
        returncode = 0
        stdout = ""
        stderr = ""

    subprocess_calls: list[dict] = []

    def fake_run(cmd, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        subprocess_calls.append({"cmd": cmd, "kwargs": kwargs})
        return FakeCompletedProcess()

    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module.subprocess, "run", fake_run)

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))

    assert len(subprocess_calls) == 1
    assert subprocess_calls[0]["cmd"][0] == worker_service_module.sys.executable
    assert result["output_path"] == str(expected_output)
    assert "command=" in str(result["performance_summary"])

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    candidate_name = str(original_filename or info.get("original_filename", "")).strip()
    preferred_stem = Path(candidate_name).stem.strip() if candidate_name else ""
    final_dir_name = preferred_stem or task_id

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / final_dir_name
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{final_dir_name}_final.mp4"
    legacy_output = task_root / f"{task_id}.mp4"

    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)
    if source.resolve() != legacy_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, legacy_output)

    archive_dir = task_root / f"{task_id}_artifacts"
    logs_dir = task_root / "logs"
    archive_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if keep_intermediate_files:
        if stage_dir.exists():
            archive_stages = archive_dir / "_stages"
            logs_stages = logs_dir / "_stages"
            if archive_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(archive_stages)
            if logs_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(logs_stages)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, archive_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, logs_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)

    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage9_organize_manifest", ".json")
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "legacy_output": str(legacy_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
        "archive_dir": str(archive_dir),
        "final_output_dir": str(task_root),
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage9_organize(*args, **kwargs)

                captured["logger"] = logger

                captured["resource_monitor"] = resource_monitor

from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path


def ensure_stage_dir(output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> Path:
    stage_dir = Path(output_dir) / task_id / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return stage_dir


def probe_duration_seconds(_input_video: str) -> float:
    # Keep this deterministic and dependency-free in the skeleton phase.
    return 0.0


def stage_artifact_path(output_dir: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, suffix: str) -> Path:
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    return stage_dir / f"{task_id}_{stage_name}{suffix}"


__all__ = ["ensure_stage_dir", "probe_duration_seconds", "stage_artifact_path"]

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def _resolve_segments(**_kwargs: Any) -> tuple[list[dict], str, str, list[dict]]:
    # Compatibility shim for tests/consumers that monkeypatch this hook.
    return ([], "timeline_fallback", "skeleton resolver", [])


def run_stage4_asr(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    hotwords: Optional[List[str]] = None,
    speaker: Optional[str] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage4 input missing")

    srt_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
    transcript_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_transcript", ".txt")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")

    engine = "stub_asr"
    sidecar_backend = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "").strip().lower()
    prefer_sidecar = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_PREFER_SIDECAR", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    sidecar_hint = Path(f"{Path(input_video).with_suffix('')}.srt")
    sidecar_raw = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", "").strip()
    sidecar_path = Path(sidecar_raw).expanduser() if sidecar_raw else sidecar_hint
    attempts: list[dict] = []

    use_sidecar = (sidecar_backend == "sidecar") or (sidecar_backend == "auto" and prefer_sidecar)
    if use_sidecar and sidecar_path.exists() and sidecar_path.is_file():
        attempts.append({"backend": "sidecar", "ok": True})
        srt_path.write_text(sidecar_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), encoding="utf-8")
        engine = "sidecar_srt"
    else:
        attempts.append({"backend": sidecar_backend or "stub", "ok": False})
        _, resolved_engine, _, _ = _resolve_segments(input_video=input_video, output_dir=output_dir, task_id=task_id)
        engine = str(resolved_engine or "timeline_fallback")
        srt_path.write_text(
            "1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nclonecut stage4 stub\n",
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

    transcript_path.write_text("clonecut stage4 transcript stub\n", encoding="utf-8")
    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_hotwords = hotwords if hotwords is not None else info.get("hotwords", [])
    if not isinstance(raw_hotwords, list):
        raw_hotwords = []
    normalized_hotwords = [str(item).strip() for item in raw_hotwords if str(item).strip()]
    dedup_hotwords: list[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in normalized_hotwords:
        if item.lower() in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(item.lower())
        dedup_hotwords.append(item)

    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    fallback_used = engine in {"timeline_fallback", "stub_asr"}
    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    result_success = not strict_rejected
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "engine": engine,
        "task_id": task_id,
        "input_video": str(source),
        "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
        "transcript_file": str(transcript_path),
        "hotwords": dedup_hotwords,
        "hotword_count": len(dedup_hotwords),
        "speaker": str(speaker or info.get("speaker", "")).strip(),
        "forum_post_info": info,
        "attempts": attempts,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

    return StageResult(
        success=result_success,
        output_file=str(source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage4 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={
            "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
            "transcript_file": str(transcript_path),
            "manifest_file": str(manifest_path),
        },
        metadata={"engine": engine},
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage4_asr(*args, **kwargs)

def _build_config(tmp_path, *, runner_mode: str = "subprocess") -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

def test_worker_service_start_and_stop_controls_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "runner_lifecycle.db"))
    events: list[str] = []

    class FakeRunner:
        def __init__(self, **_kwargs) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            events.append("runner_init")

        def start(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_start")

        def stop(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_stop")

    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "InternalPipelineWarmRunner", FakeRunner)

    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path, runner_mode="warm_process"))
    service.resource_monitor = SimpleNamespace(
        start=lambda: events.append("resource_start"),
        stop=lambda: events.append("resource_stop"),
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_recover_stuck_tasks", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_restore_retry_schedule", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_spawn_workers", lambda *_args, **_kwargs: None)

    service.start()
    service.stop()

    assert events == [
        "runner_init",
        "runner_start",
        "resource_start",
        "runner_stop",
        "resource_stop",
    ]


def test_run_internal_pipeline_prefers_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "warm_success.db"))
    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path))

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    expected_output = Path(service.config.output_dir) / "video-task-1" / "final.mp4"
    expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    expected_output.write_bytes(b"done")

    warm_calls: list[dict] = []

    class FakeRunner:
        def execute(self, *, payload, timeout_seconds):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            warm_calls.append({"payload": payload, "timeout_seconds": timeout_seconds})
            return {"success": True}

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FakeRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path", lambda **_kwargs: expected_output)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        worker_service_module.subprocess,
        "run",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("subprocess should not run")),
    )

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))

    assert len(warm_calls) == 1
    assert warm_calls[0]["payload"]["input_path"] == str(source)
    assert result["output_path"] == str(expected_output)
    assert "backend=warm_process" in str(result["performance_summary"])


def test_run_internal_pipeline_falls_back_to_subprocess_when_warm_runner_fails(
    monkeypatch,
    tmp_path,
) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "warm_fallback.db"))
    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path))

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    expected_output = Path(service.config.output_dir) / "video-task-1" / "fallback.mp4"
    expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    expected_output.write_bytes(b"done")

    class FailingRunner:
        def execute(self, *, payload, timeout_seconds):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            raise RuntimeError("warm failed")

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FailingRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module.importlib.util, "find_spec", lambda _name: object())
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path", lambda **_kwargs: expected_output)

    class FakeCompletedProcess:
        returncode = 0
        stdout = ""
        stderr = ""

    subprocess_calls: list[dict] = []

    def fake_run(cmd, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        subprocess_calls.append({"cmd": cmd, "kwargs": kwargs})
        return FakeCompletedProcess()

    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module.subprocess, "run", fake_run)

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))

    assert len(subprocess_calls) == 1
    assert subprocess_calls[0]["cmd"][0] == worker_service_module.sys.executable
    assert result["output_path"] == str(expected_output)
    assert "command=" in str(result["performance_summary"])

---
name: verification-before-completion
description: Use when about to claim work is complete, fixed, or passing, before committing or creating PRs - requires running verification commands and confirming output before making any success claims; evidence before assertions always
---

# Verification Before Completion

## Overview

Claiming work is complete without verification is dishonesty, not efficiency.

**Core principle:** Evidence before claims, always.

**Violating the letter of this rule is violating the spirit of this rule.**

## The Iron Law

```
NO COMPLETION CLAIMS WITHOUT FRESH VERIFICATION EVIDENCE
```

If you haven't run the verification command in this message, you cannot claim it passes.

## The Gate Function

```
BEFORE claiming any status or expressing satisfaction:

1. IDENTIFY: What command proves this claim?
2. RUN: Execute the FULL command (fresh, complete)
3. READ: Full output, check exit code, count failures
4. VERIFY: Does output confirm the claim?
   - If NO: State actual status with evidence
   - If YES: State claim WITH evidence
5. ONLY THEN: Make the claim

Skip any step = lying, not verifying
```

## Common Failures

| Claim | Requires | Not Sufficient |
|-------|----------|----------------|
| Tests pass | Test command output: 0 failures | Previous run, "should pass" |
| Linter clean | Linter output: 0 errors | Partial check, extrapolation |
| Build succeeds | Build command: exit 0 | Linter passing, logs look good |
| Bug fixed | Test original symptom: passes | Code changed, assumed fixed |
| Regression test works | Red-green cycle verified | Test passes once |
| Agent completed | VCS diff shows changes | Agent reports "success" |
| Requirements met | Line-by-line checklist | Tests passing |

## Red Flags - STOP

- Using "should", "probably", "seems to"
- Expressing satisfaction before verification ("Great!", "Perfect!", "Done!", etc.)
- About to commit/push/PR without verification
- Trusting agent success reports
- Relying on partial verification
- Thinking "just this once"
- Tired and wanting work over
- **ANY wording implying success without having run verification**

## Rationalization Prevention

| Excuse | Reality |
|--------|---------|
| "Should work now" | RUN the verification |
| "I'm confident" | Confidence 鈮?evidence |
| "Just this once" | No exceptions |
| "Linter passed" | Linter 鈮?compiler |
| "Agent said success" | Verify independently |
| "I'm tired" | Exhaustion 鈮?excuse |
| "Partial check is enough" | Partial proves nothing |
| "Different words so rule doesn't apply" | Spirit over letter |

## Key Patterns

**Tests:**
```
鉁?[Run test command] [See: 34/34 pass] "All tests pass"
鉂?"Should pass now" / "Looks correct"
```

**Regression tests (TDD Red-Green):**
```
鉁?Write 鈫?Run (pass) 鈫?Revert fix 鈫?Run (MUST FAIL) 鈫?Restore 鈫?Run (pass)
鉂?"I've written a regression test" (without red-green verification)
```

**Build:**
```
鉁?[Run build] [See: exit 0] "Build passes"
鉂?"Linter passed" (linter doesn't check compilation)
```

**Requirements:**
```
鉁?Re-read plan 鈫?Create checklist 鈫?Verify each 鈫?Report gaps or completion
鉂?"Tests pass, phase complete"
```

**Agent delegation:**
```
鉁?Agent reports success 鈫?Check VCS diff 鈫?Verify changes 鈫?Report actual state
鉂?Trust agent report
```

## Why This Matters

From 24 failure memories:
- your human partner said "I don't believe you" - trust broken
- Undefined functions shipped - would crash
- Missing requirements shipped - incomplete features
- Time wasted on false completion 鈫?redirect 鈫?rework
- Violates: "Honesty is a core value. If you lie, you'll be replaced."

## When To Apply

**ALWAYS before:**
- ANY variation of success/completion claims
- ANY expression of satisfaction
- ANY positive statement about work state
- Committing, PR creation, task completion
- Moving to next task
- Delegating to agents

**Rule applies to:**
- Exact phrases
- Paraphrases and synonyms
- Implications of success
- ANY communication suggesting completion/correctness

## The Bottom Line

**No shortcuts for verification.**

Run the command. Read the output. THEN claim the result.

This is non-negotiable.
